- **fund-structure-column** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-02 (PR #249 cef-scoping). Add `fund_structure` enum column to `fund_universe` ({`open_end`, `closed_end`, `etf`, `bdc`, `interval`}) ŌĆö orthogonal to `fund_strategy`. Currently structure is inferred indirectly via `series_id` prefix (SYN_ = CEF-or-open-end ambiguous, real SEC series_id = open-end), which is fragile. Lets `cross.py` and display layer make structure-aware decisions (e.g., NAV premium/discount only for `closed_end`). Workstream: investigation PR (schema design + downstream impact) ŌåÆ backfill PR (populate from SEC form-type signals) ŌåÆ display integration PR. Blockers: must follow `cef-residual-cleanup` (depends on clean SYN_ state); source-of-truth question (SEC form-type vs prospectus vs holdings shape); interaction with `fund-strategy-taxonomy-finalization`. Top exposure: VOYA $2,714B, Vanguard Group $2,541B, PIMCO $1,716B, TEACHERS ADVISORS $1,571B, TRANSAMERICA $1,303B (full top-25 in scoping doc). Q1 2026 cycle (~2026-05-15) may surface new duplicates; investigation can ship pre-cycle, population PR ships post-cycle. Sized: investigation S, population L. Critical path for Admin Refresh System institution-coverage view. **Critical-path sequencing (added post-PR #252):** Wave 1 (parallel) ŌĆö CP-1 `inst-eid-bridge-investigation` (read-only audit) + CP-3 `query4-fix-option-a` (10-line CASE rewrite at [register.py:746-750](scripts/queries/register.py:746)). Confidence-tiered manifest. **Pending.** CP-4b-author-top20 `inst-eid-bridge-author-top20` (M, pre-cycle, execution): apply CP-4b-discovery manifest pairings as new `entity_relationships` rows. **Pending ŌĆö depends on CP-4b-discovery.** Same shape as PR #249 (cef-scoping) ŌåÆ PR #251 (cef-asa-flip-and-relabel) precedent. - **pimco-13f-ingestion-gap** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-02 (PR #254 `inst-eid-bridge-investigation` ┬¦7.2). Priority: P2. **Problem.** PIMCO does not file 13F under any entity present in `holdings_v2`. CIK `0001163368` (PACIFIC INVESTMENT MANAGEMENT CO LLC, `eid=2322`) is the canonical PIMCO US adviser registration but is absent from `holdings_v2.cik` entirely. `eid=30` (PIMCO name-only) and `eid=2322` both carry $0 filer AUM. Allianz parent entities (`eid=1358`, `eid=589`) carry filer AUM but the totals ($20.4B + $348.4B) cannot account for PIMCO's expected $1.7T US equity rollup. **Diagnosis hypotheses:** (1) form-13F-NT filtering excludes PIMCO's filings during ingestion; (2) Allianz parent-rollup logic absorbs PIMCO filings into a parent eid; (3) known-broken filer pattern in `load_13f_v2.py`. **Workstream:** investigation-first, fix-second. Investigation PR (S) ŌĆö read SEC EDGAR for PIMCO 13F filings, cross-reference against `load_13f_v2.py` ingestion logic, identify why PIMCO CIK is absent. Fix PR (sized after investigation). **Out of scope:** brand-vs-filer bridge for `eid=30` ŌåÆ `eid=2322` (handled by CP-4a per `inst_eid_bridge_decisions.md`).
- **fund-strategy-taxonomy-finalization** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-01 (PR-4 follow-up). Review and finalize the five edge categories in the canonical `fund_strategy` taxonomy. Several values were inherited from the original classifier and carry vague labels or arbitrary boundaries that do not survive scrutiny: (1) **`balanced`** (60-90% equity composition) ŌĆö vague label, boundary with `multi_asset` is arbitrary; decide keep as composition-based bucket / rename to `active_equity_heavy` / merge into `active`; (2) **`multi_asset`** (30-60% equity composition) ŌĆö boundaries with `balanced` (60%) and `bond_or_other` (30%) are both arbitrary thresholds; decide keep distinct / merge with `balanced` / rename; (3) **`bond_or_other`** ŌĆö heterogeneous bucket; the `saba-proshares-reclassify` 2026-05-01 PR moved 39 ProShares short / inverse / leveraged-short funds out of this bucket to `passive` (closing the bucket's largest miscategorisation); residual is bond funds + niche cases. Could still split into `bond` and `inverse_or_short` if a richer taxonomy is preferred ŌĆö but the urgency is gone now that ProShares is corrected; (4) **`excluded`** ŌĆö combines money markets, fund-of-funds, and ETF wrappers that skip classification; should split into specific reasons; (5) **`final_filing`** ŌĆö status flag, not a strategy; 12+ funds (the 12 BlackRock muni trusts, all confirmed merged Feb 2026 by the `fund-cleanup-batch` 2026-05-01 audit, plus other final-filing rows); decide whether this belongs in `fund_strategy` at all or should become a separate `is_terminating` boolean. Output: findings doc with row counts per category, decisions list, recommended target taxonomy. Trigger: orphan/NULL data is now on the table (`fund-cleanup-batch` 2026-05-01 audit closed `canonical-value-coverage-audit`); residual orphan disposition tracked under `fund-holdings-orphan-investigation` and `historical-fund-holdings-drift-audit`. The merge/split decisions can now be staged.
- **canonical-value-coverage-audit** ŌĆö broader audit of NULL `fund_strategy`, orphan series, edge cohorts (UNKNOWN orphans / SYN drifters / BlackRock muni trusts), 3-way `CASE` NULL semantics in `cross.py`, and rows where `fund_holdings_v2.fund_strategy_at_filing` differs from `fund_universe.fund_strategy`. **Status (2026-05-01 conv-24):** Phase 1 (data-pull / row-count + AUM exposure across canonical buckets) was executed inside `fund-cleanup-batch` (PR #242); see `docs/findings/fund_cleanup_batch_results.md` ┬¦1aŌĆō┬¦1h. The structured per-bucket count + AUM exposure + recommended treatment table is the still-open deliverable; the SYN drift cohort + 301-series orphan cohort + 3-way CASE NULL semantics review remain to be characterized end-to-end. Trigger: next architectural session that picks up `fund-strategy-taxonomy-finalization`.
- **index-benchmark-validation** ŌĆö Systematize fund-to-index classification using N-PORT holdings data. Builds on the one-off Item 8 work from 2026-04-09 (existing `index_proxies` / `fund_index_scores` / `benchmark_weights` tables) by turning it into a maintained pipeline. Coverage findings: `docs/findings/index_benchmark_coverage.md`. **Phase 1 ŌĆö Index reference table:** 27 benchmarks identified from `fund_universe` naming (S&P 500: 227 funds / $4.0T; Total Stock Market: 14 / $2.7T; Nasdaq 100: 98 / $579B; plus sector + international). Pick one representative fund per benchmark as the reference portfolio (e.g. Vanguard 500 Index for S&P 500). Store as `benchmark_portfolios(benchmark_name, series_id, quarter, ticker, weight)` ŌĆö supersedes `index_proxies` once parity verified. **Phase 2 ŌĆö Correlation scoring pipeline:** for each fund in `fund_holdings_v2`, compute overlap % and weight correlation against each benchmark. Store as `fund_index_correlation(series_id, benchmark_name, quarter, overlap_pct, weight_corr)` ŌĆö supersedes `fund_index_scores`. Rules: >90% overlap + >0.95 weight corr ŌćÆ confirmed passive; <60% overlap ŌćÆ confirmed active; middle ŌćÆ review. **Phase 3 ŌĆö Unmatched fund classification:** 3,599 funds with "Index"/"ETF" in name ($4.6T) remain unmatched to a specific benchmark; correlation against the reference portfolios will classify them. Periodic weight validation against external sources (S&P factsheets). **Phase 4 ŌĆö Sector fund integration:** 11 GICS sector benchmarks identified (Tech $151B, Health Care $63B, Financials $70B, Energy $49B, etc.); incorporate sector fund compositions into Sector Rotation tab. Priority: Medium. Prerequisite: none. Depends on: N-PORT data (available). Blocks: improved active/passive accuracy on all tabs.

The Register tab applies four different "active" predicates across read sites: [register.py:1018](scripts/queries/register.py:1018) excludes activists from the active universe; [register.py:472](scripts/queries/register.py:472), [register.py:1354](scripts/queries/register.py:1354), and [market.py:373/498](scripts/queries/market.py:373) include them. Same tab, same conceptual filter, four different SQL predicates ŌĆö active-universe size depends on which endpoint a UI element calls. Two-PR workstream: investigation PR (S, confirm the four sites, document the intended canonical definition, surface any other read sites with the same shape) ŌåÆ fix PR (S, single canonical helper, all four sites migrate to it, no data writes). **Sequencing: must ship BEFORE any activist-as-flag refactor** ŌĆö the flag refactor depends on a single canonical active-universe definition existing first. Out of scope: the activist-as-flag schema migration itself (separate workstream from PR #252 Phase 5).

- **cp-5-fof-subtraction-cusip-linkage** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-06 (PR #299 `cp-5-1b-helper-and-view` Phase 2). Priority: P2. **Problem.** The `unified_holdings` view ships without the intra-family fund-of-fund subtraction Bundle A ┬¦1.4 specified for the modified-R5 rule, because the data model has no canonical CUSIPŌåÆfund-entity bridge: fund entities carry `series_id` and rare `cik` in `entity_identifiers`, not CUSIP, and `securities` has no `entity_id` linkage. The intra-family FoF CTE prototyped in PR #299 matched zero rows for every firm including Vanguard. **Workstream.** Build a canonical CUSIPŌåÆfund-entity bridge. Likely paths: (a) populate `securities.entity_id` for fund-issued securities by matching against `fund_universe.fund_cik`; (b) translate `ncen_adviser_map.series_id` to fund-issued CUSIPs; (c) match `securities.issuer_name ILIKE fund_name` (brittle, last resort). Once bridge exists, re-add the `intra_family_fof` CTE to `unified_holdings`. **Out of scope.** Single-quarter parameterization of `unified_holdings` (separate workstream). **Refs:** `docs/findings/cp-5-1b-helper-and-view-results.md` ┬¦4, `docs/decisions/inst_eid_bridge_decisions.md` Modified R5 section.

### P3 ŌĆö Quick wins / low priority

- **source-type-value-canonicalization** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-02 (PR #255 `ingestion-manifest-reconcile` Appendix A ┬¦A.5; entry confirmed in CP-4a chat 2026-05-02). `ingestion_manifest.source_type` writes use two different value conventions: direct writes (e.g. legacy paths) emit `'NPORT'` while SourcePipeline-base writes emit `'nport_holdings'` (sourced from `PIPELINE_CADENCE.keys()` in `scripts/pipeline/`). The mismatch affects `admin_bp.py:1346` last-run lookup ŌĆö admin dashboard last-run cards may miss a recent run if the lookup keys on one convention but the most recent write used the other. Workstream: audit all `source_type` writes to enumerate the two conventions, decide canonical value per pipeline (likely `'nport_holdings'` for the SourcePipeline-aligned set, plus a one-time UPDATE to backfill any direct writes onto the canonical convention), patch any remaining direct-write call sites, then update `admin_bp.py:1346` lookup. Single S PR. Parallel to critical path (no dependency on `inst-eid-bridge` or `parent-level-display-canonical-reads`). Out of scope for the original CP-2 PR per the bias-toward-DROP rule (scope was schema-name reconcile, not value-name reconcile).

- **stage-b-turnover-deferred-funds** ŌĆö Three Vanguard funds and similar individual cases are passive in behavior but their names do not match systemic INDEX_PATTERNS rules: Vanguard Primecap (~$76B), Vanguard Windsor II (~$65B), Vanguard Equity Income (~$62B). These will be flagged for reclassification by Stage B (position turnover detection) which validates passive behavior via holdings stability rather than name regex. Total ~$203B AUM affected. Adjacent case: Bridgeway Ultra-Small Company Market (~$0.13B) ŌĆö passive Bridgeway-internal index tracker that the PR-2 sweep deliberately did not catch (the `\bUltra\b` pattern was rejected because of false positives on actively-managed Ultra-named funds, and `\bBridgeway\b` is mixed-purpose). Surfaced 2026-05-01 (PR-2 follow-up); demoted from P2 ŌåÆ P3 in `conv-24-doc-sync` because the trigger (Stage B turnover detection design) is itself a separate, larger initiative not yet on this roadmap. Trigger: Stage B turnover detection design.

- **worktree-cleanup-hygiene-cadence** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-04 (`conv-28-doc-sync`, succeeds completed `worktree-cleanup-hygiene` PR #274). Priority: P3 recurring. **Trigger.** Re-run the worktree-cleanup-hygiene workflow whenever orphan worktrees + branches accumulate above ~5 entries. Per PR #274 ┬¦7.5, the `gh pr merge --delete-branch` failure pattern is permanent (the flag silently no-ops on remote when a worktree holds the branch at merge time) ŌĆö manual cadence cleanup is structural, not transient. Pattern: `git worktree remove --force` retired worktrees ŌåÆ `git branch -d` (IN-MAIN) / `-D` (squash-merged) ŌåÆ `git push origin --delete <branch>` for orphan remote branches. Adjacent to `repo-branch-hygiene` but specific to the worktree dimension. **Out of scope:** worktrees with unpushed work (per-worktree decision required).
- **repo-branch-hygiene** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-02 (sync-audit, commit `7f21574`). Priority: P3. **Problem.** ~15 stale `claude/*` local branches and ~120 remote branches have accumulated. None are operationally impeding, but periodic cleanup is good hygiene. **Workstream:** single S Code session ŌĆö enumerate squash-merged branches, prune local + remote. Run when convenient or when stale branches actively impede a workflow. **Out of scope:** ad-hoc cleanup of branches with unpushed work (those need per-branch decisions).
- **fund-cik-entity-type-audit** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-05 (`cp-5-loader-gap-remediation-sub1` ┬¦1.6). Priority: P3 post-CP-5. **Problem.** All 23 LINKABLE targets in the sub-PR 1 manifest carry `entity_type='institution'` rather than `'fund'`, despite each being a per-fund registrant CIK with a 1:1 CIK linkage and per-fund canonical name (Bond Fund of America, Tax Exempt Bond Fund of America, etc.). Two possible explanations: (a) intentional convention ŌĆö the N-PORT loader treats registrant-CIK entities as institutions, with fund-tier identity carried in `fund_universe` rows; (b) loader bug ŌĆö the entities should be `'fund'` and have been mis-typed at seed time. **Workstream.** Read-only audit script: enumerate every entity reachable from `entity_identifiers.identifier_type='cik'` whose CIK ALSO appears in `fund_universe.fund_cik`; bucket by `entities.entity_type`; characterize the shape (1:1 vs N:1 CIK linkage, ECH classification, presence of `fund_universe` row, presence of an upstream sponsor/adviser bridge in `entity_relationships`). If the dominant pattern is `entity_type='institution'` and the convention is intentional, document the contract explicitly. If the convention is a loader artifact, scope a typing-correction migration as a separate PR. **Decision deferral.** Don't act in conv-30 doc-sync ŌĆö defer to chat after CP-5.1 ships. **Out of scope.** No mutations; no retro-typing; no impact on CP-5 critical path (Method A JOIN does not filter by `entity_type`). **Trigger.** Schedule after CP-5.1 reader migrations land.

Other non-cycle entities in the same neighborhood may carry similar shape (control edge to a recently-merged eid, but not duplicate-merge candidates themselves). **Workstream.** Read-only audit walking each merged canonical's neighborhood to identify cycle-adjacent eids, characterize their shape, and decide if any need follow-up bridges. **Decision deferral.** Don't act in conv-30 doc-sync ŌĆö defer to chat after CP-5.1 ships. **Out of scope.** No mutations.
- **entity-current-inverted-rollup-audit** ŌĆö Surfaced 2026-05-05 (`cp-5-adams-duplicates` PR #283 Op H Branch 2). ## Known issues

- ~~**fund_strategy classification drift**~~ ŌĆö RESOLVED 2026-05-01 by the PR-2 / PR-4 sequence. (1) PR-2 added the pipeline write-path lock (`_apply_fund_strategy_lock` + `_upsert_fund_universe` COALESCE in [scripts/pipeline/load_nport.py](scripts/pipeline/load_nport.py)); once a series carries a non-NULL `fund_strategy`, subsequent classifier outputs are discarded. (2) PR-4 changed the only remaining query-layer reader of point-in-time holdings (`compute_peer_rotation.py:_materialize_fund_agg`) to LEFT JOIN `fund_universe.fund_strategy` instead of reading `fund_holdings_v2.fund_strategy_at_filing` (column renamed in the same PR). With both legs landed the per-quarter drift class is structurally impossible. The historical mismatch between `fund_universe.fund_strategy` and `fund_holdings_v2.fund_strategy_at_filing` is preserved in the `_at_filing` column (snapshot semantics, intentional) and was quantified 2026-05-01 by the `fund-cleanup-batch` audit (40,843 latest-only divergent rows; see `docs/findings/fund_cleanup_batch_results.md` ┬¦1g). Residual non-SYN drift (~31,400 rows) carried as P3 `historical-fund-holdings-drift-audit`.

## Architectural locks

- **Two-canonical-classifications (locked 2026-05-03 via fund-typed-ech-cleanup arc, PRs #262ŌĆō#265).**
  - Institution ŌåÆ `entity_classification_history.classification` (canonical reader: `entity_current.classification`).
  - Fund ŌåÆ `fund_universe.fund_strategy` (canonical reader bridge: `classify_fund_strategy()` in `scripts/queries/common.py`, added in PR #264).
  - Reads route by `entity_type`. ECH carries zero open fund-typed rows after PR #265 (13,220-row SCD close).
  - Both classifications are determined once, frozen, and not revisited on refresh. Writer paths gated against fund-typed targets in PR #263.
  - Refs `docs/decisions/d4-classification-precedence.md`, `docs/findings/fund-typed-ech-audit.md`. Critical-path consumer: CP-5 `parent-level-display-canonical-reads` wraps the helper.
- **BLOCKER 2 carve-out (locked 2026-05-03 via PR #269 addendum).** The strict-ADV cross-ref rule for brand-vs-filer bridging (BLOCKER 2 in `inst_eid_bridge_decisions.md`) stays. Narrow exception: brands corroborated by 2+ orthogonal signals OR Bucket C with raw-string identical aliases (X2 alone) AND public-record verification qualify as `AUTHOR_NEW_BRIDGE`-eligible at MEDIUM confidence. Carve-out applied to the cp-4b arc (4 brands / ~$2,055.4B bridged across PRs #267, #269, #270, #271); 15 LOW-cohort brands / ~$10.27T residual deferred to the post-CP-5 cp-4c brand-bridges backlog (#20 in `data/working/cp-5-execution-plan.csv`). Refs `docs/decisions/inst_eid_bridge_decisions.md`, `docs/findings/cp-4b-blocker2-corroboration-probe.md`.
- **CP-5 institutional rollup read layer (locked 2026-05-04 via PRs [#277](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/277)ŌĆō[#281](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/281)).** 8 design decisions:
  - **R5 Dedup Rule.** For each `(top_parent, ticker, cusip)` triple in 2025Q4: `result = MAX(thirteen_f, fund_tier_adjusted)` where `fund_tier_adjusted` excludes intra-family FoF (~$2,207B) and non-valid-CUSIP rows (EC asset_category only, ~$5,172B). Source-winner tag (`13F_wins` / `fund_wins`); `13F_only` and `fund_only` top-parents handled explicitly. See `docs/findings/cp-5-comprehensive-remediation.md` ┬¦2.1.
  - **Method A canonical (climb mechanism).** Read-time JOIN against `entity_rollup_history erh ON erh.entity_id = fh.entity_id AND erh.rollup_type = 'decision_maker_v1' AND erh.valid_to = '9999-12-31'`, then climb `inst_to_top_parent` from `erh.rollup_entity_id`. Method B (`fund_holdings_v2.dm_rollup_entity_id` denormalized at load time) is **not** canonical ŌĆö goes stale after every ERH rebuild (live evidence: SSGA cp-4b bridge surfaced $778.2B Method AŌåöB drift). Method B's residual role is as a cache-invalidation signal. See ┬¦2.2.
  - **decision_maker_v1 canonical for institutional view (View 1).** `entity_rollup_history.rollup_type='decision_maker_v1'` is canonical. `economic_control_v1` retained for parallel sponsor-view queries. 13.8% of funds have `dm ŌēĀ ec` rollup; for BlackRock Inc. the choice swings fund-tier AUM by 27%. See ┬¦2.3.
  - **Time-versioning Option C (hybrid).** `entity_relationships` schema already supports SCD via `valid_from` / `valid_to`. Today's graph is time-invariant (378 of 395 instŌåÆinst control rows have default `valid_from = 2000-01-01`). When historical (pre-2025) data loads, capture 20ŌĆō30 known M&A events as explicit `valid_from` overrides per the existing SCD schema. Not a CP-5 execution dependency ŌĆö defer M&A event register to Pipeline 4+ scope. See ┬¦2.4.
  - **View 2 scope.** Tier 1 = N-PORT-filing registered funds (1,954 funds / $31.6T EC) ŌĆö full PM-level decomposition; Tier 2 = 13D/G partial (>5% positions, non-N-PORT filers) ŌĆö surface as "PM partial" with caveat; Tier 3 = hedge fund / SMA / pension / family / SWF / VC / activist / endowment ($4.9T 13F across 1,367 filers) ŌĆö institutional-tier with explicit "no fund decomposition available" sentinel flag. See ┬¦2.7.
  - **Two-canonical-classifications** (locked 2026-05-03; reaffirmed Bundle A ┬¦2.4) ŌĆö institution ŌåÆ `entity_classification_history`; fund ŌåÆ `fund_universe.fund_strategy`. Reaffirmed by zero NULL `fund_strategy` in `fund_universe`.
  - **Operating-AM rollup policy** (memory rule + Bundle B ┬¦2.5) ŌĆö rollup terminates at the operating asset manager; never at bank/insurance/holding-co parent. 3ŌĆō4 candidate violations covering ~$2.78T 13F (BoA, RBC, BNY Mellon, Manulife) ŌĆö defer to post-CP-5 (#18 in execution plan).
  - **BLOCKER 2 carve-out** (locked 2026-05-03 per PR #269 addendum) ŌĆö reference only; already in effect (see lock above).
  - Refs `docs/findings/cp-5-comprehensive-remediation.md` (full design contract), `data/working/cp-5-execution-plan.csv` (26-PR dependency sequence).

---

## Process rules

- **Audit-prompt design rule ŌĆö sum-identity over ratio-bound** (locked 2026-05-04 via PR [#279](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/279) `cp-5-coverage-matrix-revalidation`). When computing pre/post numerical deltas across a cohort with non-uniform per-row inflation factors, prefer sum-identity gates (`|orig ŌłÆ sum(parts)| Ōēż ╬Ą`) over ratio-bound gates (e.g., `a/b Ōłł [0.95, 2.05]`). Sum-identity holds exactly across heterogeneous data; ratio bounds trip on legitimate per-entity variance. The PR #279 STOP gate tripped on BlackRock (1.73├Ś) and Fidelity (2.04├Ś) under a ratio gate; the sum-identity replacement passed exactly across all firms. Apply to any future audit that compares aggregated cohorts before/after a transformation.
- **DuckDB DROP COLUMN with PRIMARY KEY ŌĆö CTAS-and-swap** (locked 2026-05-05 via PR [#296](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/296) `cp-5-holdings-v2-dm-rollup-drop`). DuckDB has no `ALTER TABLE DROP CONSTRAINT`. When dropping a column from a table that carries a `PRIMARY KEY`, plain `ALTER TABLE DROP COLUMN` fails ŌĆö the implicit PK index sits on a column positioned after the dropped one. Use the CTAS-and-swap pattern: drop indexes; `CREATE TABLE <new> AS SELECT * EXCLUDE (...)` from the old; `DROP TABLE <old>`; `ALTER TABLE <new> RENAME TO <old>`; `ADD CONSTRAINT ... PRIMARY KEY (...)`; recreate indexes verbatim. Reference: `scripts/migrations/025_drop_holdings_v2_dm_rollup_denorm.py` (PR #296) and `scripts/migrations/026_drop_bo_v2_dm_rollup_denorm.py` (this PR).
- **Audit pipeline readers when scoping schema drops** (locked 2026-05-05 via PR [#296](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/296)). Reader audits must include `scripts/pipeline/`, `scripts/compute_*`, `scripts/build_*`, and any other recompute paths ŌĆö not just `scripts/queries/` + `scripts/api_*.py`. PR #296 caught 5 pipeline readers that PR #295's user-facing-only audit missed (`compute_flows`, `build_summaries`, `compute_peer_rotation`, `compute_parent_fund_map`, `build_fixture`). Leaving them would have broken the next pipeline run, not the next request. Future schema-drop PRs grep all of `scripts/`.
- **New entities need both rollup types at creation** (locked 2026-05-05 via PRs [#291](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/291) + [#293](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/293)). Every new-entity PR must `INSERT` self-rollup rows for **both** `decision_maker_v1` AND `economic_control_v1` ŌĆö `entity_current` sources `rollup_entity_id` from `economic_control_v1`, so an entity missing the EC self-rollup is invisible to that view. Capital Group umbrella (PR #287, Path A) reused a long-standing eid that already carries both. Loader-gap remediation sub-PR 2 (PR #291) added Op E2 to insert both rows inline at creation; PR #293 audited PR #287 to confirm both rollup types were present. Future entity-creation PRs follow the PR #291 inline pattern.
- **`entity_identifiers` schema ŌĆö no `is_preferred` column** (locked 2026-05-05 via PR [#291](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/291)). `entity_identifiers` uses `confidence` / `source` / `is_inferred` instead of `is_preferred`. The `is_preferred` field lives on `entity_aliases`. Earlier prompts that referenced `entity_identifiers.is_preferred` were authored from the alias-table mental model. Reference: PR #291 in-flight refinement (bootstrap_tier4 precedent).

---

## cef-residual-cleanup

**Status:** **CLOSED 2026-05-02** ┬Ę **Priority:** P2 ┬Ę **Surfaced:** PR [#247](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/247) (BRANCH 2 holdouts) ┬Ę **Reframed:** PR [#249](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/249) (cef-scoping) ┬Ę **Closed:** PR-A #250 + PR-B `cef-asa-flip-and-relabel`

**Problem.** 446 rows / $4.741B in `fund_holdings_v2` under `series_id='UNKNOWN'` from 2 CEF CIKs (Adams Diversified Equity Fund `0000002230`, ASA Gold & Precious Metals `0001230869`). Per PR #249 scoping: this is migration-015 residue from the retired loader `scripts/retired/fetch_nport.py`, NOT a CEF architecture gap. CEFs file N-PORT under Rule 30b1-9 and the `SYN_<cik>` namespace already correctly loads 436 of 438 CEFs in `fund_holdings_v2` ($625.94B AUM).

Decision per PR #249: keep `SYN_<cik>` as canonical CEF identifier (Option C ŌĆö status quo). Skip historical N-CSR backfill (Parser Option D). Net new modern data over N-PORT = 0; ~3ŌĆō5 weeks effort if ever pursued. Original 4-PR follow-on arc (cef-fetch-pipeline, cef-parser, cef-holdings-load, display integration) DROPPED.

### Workstream sequence (revised, ~1ŌĆō2 sessions)

- ~~**PR-A `cef-residual-cleanup-adx`** (S) ŌĆö flip 96 ADX byte-identical duplicates to `is_latest=FALSE`.~~ **Landed 2026-05-02.** Single-period cohort (2025-09-30); 96/96 byte-identical to `SYN_0000002230` companions; 0 mismatches; 0 orphans. Global `series_id='UNKNOWN' AND is_latest=TRUE` 446 ŌåÆ 350.
- ~~**PR-B `cef-asa-flip-and-relabel`** (S) ŌĆö flip 350 ASA UNKNOWN rows to `is_latest=FALSE` and relabel to `series_id='SYN_0001230869'`.~~ **Landed 2026-05-02.** 350/350 byte-identical to ASA's N-PORT filings ($0.00 per-period delta); single-tx INSERT 350 SYN + UPDATE 350 UNKNOWN; AUM conservation ╬ö = $0.00. Fund-attribution override (entity_id 11278 ŌåÆ 26793, dm_rollup_name 'Calamos Investments' ŌåÆ 'ASA Gold and Precious Metals LTD Fund') applied per chat decision; mirrors existing 2025-11 SYN row. Global `series_id='UNKNOWN' AND is_latest=TRUE` 350 ŌåÆ 0. Workstream closes.

### Out of scope

- N-CSR / NSAR holdings parsing (resolved by PR #249: not needed).
- BDC (Form 10-K), interval funds ŌĆö separate workstreams.

### Revision history

- **2026-05-02** ŌĆö PR-B reframed from `cef-asa-period-backfill` (M, fetch+load+flip) to `cef-asa-flip-and-relabel` (S, flip+relabel) per `docs/findings/cef_asa_prep_investigation.md` (commit `79350a5`). Investigation found ASA UNKNOWN rows are byte-identical ($0.00 delta) to the corresponding NPORT-P filings already on EDGAR, so the data is already in `fund_holdings_v2` ŌĆö only the `series_id` label is wrong. v2 loader rerun would create rows under `1230869_<accession>` (CEFs report `series_id=None`), inconsistent with the existing 2025-11 `SYN_0001230869` row.

## fund-structure-column

**Status:** Open ┬Ę **Priority:** P2 ┬Ę **Surfaced:** PR [#249](https://github.com/ST5555-Code/Institutional-Ownership/pull/249) (cef-scoping)

**Problem.** `fund_universe.fund_strategy` describes investment style (active, passive, etc.) but does not capture fund structure. CEFs trade at premium/discount to NAV; open-end funds do not. ETFs, BDCs, and interval funds each behave differently in display layer. Currently structure is inferred indirectly via `series_id` prefix (`SYN_` = CEF-or-open-end ambiguous, real SEC `series_id` = open-end), which is fragile.

**Proposal.** Add `fund_structure` enum column to `fund_universe`: `{open_end, closed_end, etf, bdc, interval}`. Orthogonal to `fund_strategy`. Lets `cross.py` and display layer make structure-aware decisions (e.g., show NAV premium/discount only for `closed_end`).

### Workstream shape (estimated)

- **Investigation PR** ŌĆö schema design, migration plan, downstream query impact analysis.
- **Backfill PR** ŌĆö populate `fund_structure` for all existing `fund_universe` rows from SEC form-type signals.
- **Display integration PR** ŌĆö surface in relevant tabs.

### Blockers

- Must follow `cef-residual-cleanup` (depends on clean `SYN_` state).
- Source-of-truth question: SEC form-type, fund prospectus, or derived from holdings shape?
- Interaction with `fund-strategy-taxonomy-finalization` (separate P2 workstream).

**Out of scope:** `nav_per_share` enrichment (deferred ŌĆö no current analytic depends on it).

| 2026-04-30 | **sr-fund-quarter-filter (PR #215)** | Two enhancements to Sector Rotation Fund view. New `GET /api/v1/fund_quarter_completeness` returns per-quarter `months_available` + `complete` flag (true iff 3 N-PORT report-months filed) from `fund_holdings_v2`; tab fetches once on mount and filters out incomplete destination quarters from the sector heatmap when `level='fund'`. Institution view + the static Net Flows heatmap unaffected. New `GET /api/v1/sector_monthly_flows?sector=&quarter=` computes monthly net flows from paired filers (funds present in both current and prior month); months are derived from data because N-PORT report-months trail the filing quarter by one period (quarter='2026Q1' contains report_months 2025-10/11/12); funds present in only one month are excluded since most filers report only at quarter-end and treating a missing month as an exit produced spurious trillion-dollar swings. Heatmap tooltip lazy-fetches per (sector, quarter), caches in component state, shows "Loading monthly detailŌĆ”" while in-flight, renders abbreviated month labels in JetBrains Mono with green/red semantic colors per DarkStyle.md. The pipeline T2 tier (`build_cusip` / `build_managers` / `load_13f` / `unify_positions` / `compute_flows` / `fetch_adv` / `fetch_13dg`) is out of scope here and remains documented in `docs/write_path_risk_map.md`; future BL-3-shaped work belongs in those pipeline-touch sessions. No code changes ŌĆö the audit is the deliverable. **(B) INF53 ŌĆö BACKFILL_MIG015 multi-row root cause.** Read `scripts/migrations/015_amendment_semantics.py:181-202` (`fund_holdings_v2` migrator: bulk additive UPDATE setting `accession_number = 'BACKFILL_MIG015_' \|\| series_id \|\| '_' \|\| report_month`, never dedupes). Sampled 5 BACKFILL real-CUSIP groups + 3 NPORT_NORMAL real-CUSIP groups + 1 fake-series cusip='N/A' group (Stone Ridge Alternative Lending) from `data/reports/inf51/value_divergent_groups_20260427_192000.csv`. **By design.** N-PORT lets a fund report multiple `<invstOrSec>` line items per security per filing ŌĆö observed patterns: (i) Long+Short hedged pairs (Franklin Alternative Strategies, CUSIP 31935HAD9, n=3); (ii) multiple Long lots / sub-portfolios with no business-axis tie-breaker (iShares Core US Agg Bond ETF ŌĆö 3├Ś STIV repo positions $100K + $735M + $4.5B); (iii) placeholder-CUSIP buckets aggregating distinct non-CUSIP holdings (Stone Ridge ŌĆö 210,484 of 210,535 rows are `asset_category='LON'` with internal loan IDs as `issuer_name`, all `cusip='N/A'`). 1,551 NPORT_NORMAL groups exhibit the same pattern with real accessions, so the multi-row shape is intrinsic to N-PORT, not an artifact of MIG015. Distinguishing-axis breakdown: `payoff_profile` resolves only 397 / 1,551 NPORT_NORMAL groups (25.6%); 1,154 (74.4%) have multiple positions on the same payoff side. The actual PK is the surrogate `row_id BIGINT` (already enforced via `fund_holdings_v2_row_id_pkey` in migration `020_pk_enforcement.py`); `(series_id, report_month, accession_number, cusip)` was never a natural key. **No fix.** Recommendation: (a) note in PK-assumption docs that this tuple is non-unique; (b) analytic dedup uses `SUM(shares_or_principal)` / `SUM(market_value_usd)` across the group, optionally filtered by `payoff_profile='Long'` ŌĆö already the convention in current rollup queries; (c) future N-PORT line-item ordinal column is non-blocking. Findings doc: `docs/findings/inf53-backfill-mig015-multirow.md`. No DB writes, no schema changes. |

| 2026-04-27 | **inf50-52-nport-pipeline-fixes** | Code-only hardening of `scripts/pipeline/load_nport.py` for the two pipeline bugs surfaced during 2026-04-27 `nport-refresh-catchup` (logged as INF52 in P2 + as an unnumbered observation for the silent cleanup). **INF50 ŌĆö `_cleanup_staging` silent failure.** Prior implementation called `super()._cleanup_staging(run_id)` (which DROPped `fund_holdings_v2` typed staging in its own connection), then opened a SECOND staging writer to DROP `stg_nport_holdings` + `stg_nport_fund_universe`, with the whole second block wrapped in `except Exception ŌåÆ self._logger.warning`. Any failure in the second connection (file lock, DROP no-op, etc.) was swallowed; that's how Apr 15 DERA Session 2 promote left 11.1M rows in `stg_nport_holdings` that nearly contaminated the Apr 27 topup (parse() does `INSERT INTO fund_holdings_v2 ... SELECT ... FROM stg_nport_holdings` with no `loaded_at` filter). **Fix:** rewrote `_cleanup_staging` to drop all three tables (`fund_holdings_v2` + `stg_nport_holdings` + `stg_nport_fund_universe`) on a single staging writer connection, and added a post-cleanup assertion ŌĆö for each table, attempt `SELECT COUNT(*)`; a `duckdb.CatalogException` is the success signal (table absent), any other outcome `raise RuntimeError(f"...{t} still exists with {rows} rows after DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ŌĆö staging is contaminated...")`. Removed the broad `except ŌåÆ warning`; cleanup now fails LOUDLY in `approve_and_promote`. **Pre-fetch guard:** new `_purge_stale_raw_staging` helper called at the start of `fetch()` after `_ensure_staging_schema`. For each raw staging table, reads `COUNT(*)`; if `> 0`, logs a WARNING with the count and runs `DELETE FROM <t>` so leftover rows from a prior silent-failed cleanup never reach parse(). **INF52 ŌĆö int-23 guard vs entity enrichment ordering.** `LoadNPortPipeline.parse` (line 731-734) intentionally NULLs `entity_id` / `rollup_entity_id` / `dm_entity_id` / `dm_rollup_entity_id` / `dm_rollup_name`; `_bulk_enrich_run` populated them AFTER `super().promote()` returned. The int-23 downgrade-refusal guard inside `_promote_append_is_latest` (`base.py:631`, `_DOWNGRADE_SENSITIVE_COLUMNS = ("ticker", "entity_id", "rollup_entity_id")`) fired BEFORE the post-promote enrich, refused to flip is_latest on (series, month) keys where prod had populated entity columns, and rolled back the whole promote. **Fix:** new `_enrich_staging_entities(prod_con, series_touched)` method that mirrors `_bulk_enrich_run`'s JOIN against `entity_identifiers` + `entity_rollup_history` (EC + DM) + `entity_aliases`, fetches the mapping into a pandas DataFrame on the existing `prod_con` (no second connection), then opens a fresh staging writer and runs `UPDATE staging.fund_holdings_v2 SET entity_id, rollup_entity_id, dm_entity_id, dm_rollup_entity_id, dm_rollup_name FROM entity_map m WHERE fh.series_id = m.series_id`, CHECKPOINT, close. Wired into `LoadNPortPipeline.promote()` as step 0, BEFORE `super().promote()` runs. Step ordering documented in the docstring as `enrich ŌåÆ promote ŌåÆ re-enrich (safety net)`. `_bulk_enrich_run` continues to run post-promote ŌĆö idempotent, no-ops on already-filled rows, catches the rare case where MDM state shifts between pre-enrich and promote. Test fixture + incomplete-prod-schema robustness: pre-enrich's prod-side fetch is wrapped in `except Exception ŌåÆ warning, return 0` (post-promote `_bulk_enrich_run` uses the same pattern); the int-23 guard still catches real downgrades, so a swallowed pre-enrich at most degrades gracefully to the prior behavior (and surfaces the underlying prod issue via the warning). **Tests:** 6 new unit tests in `tests/pipeline/test_load_nport.py`. INF50: (a) `_cleanup_staging` drops all 3 tables (CatalogException on post-DROP SELECT for each); (b) monkeypatched `DuckDBPyConnection.execute` no-ops on `DROP TABLE` ŌåÆ `_cleanup_staging` raises `RuntimeError` matching `"staging is contaminated"`; (c) `_purge_stale_raw_staging` clears stale rows from both raw tables. INF52: (a) seeds prod entity tables with eid=42 / EC-rollup=100 / DM-rollup=200 / alias="Test Family", parses staging with NULL entity columns, calls `_enrich_staging_entities`, asserts all 5 columns populated correctly; (b) empty `series_touched` returns 0 without exception; (c) absent `entity_*` tables in prod produces a warning + return 0 (no raise). All 22 nport tests pass (16 original + 6 new); full `tests/smoke/` + `tests/pipeline/` 230/230 pass. Pre-commit clean (ruff + pylint + bandit; tracker-staleness skipped ŌĆö no .md changes in this commit's first pass, refreshed in the doc-sync edit). **No DB writes, no schema changes, no migration.** Pipeline behavior unchanged on the green path; failure modes for both bugs now surface immediately in the next pipeline run instead of silently degrading. |

Latency parent **335-405ms ŌåÆ 22-36ms** (~12├Ś); target was <200ms. Parity: top-5 buyer/seller institution rankings match exactly, every per-institution `net_flow` matches to 0.0000%, `summary.net` / `summary.buyers` / `summary.sellers` match exactly. Known divergence: `summary.inflow` / `summary.outflow` and per-institution `buying` / `selling` shift ~1.1% because `peer_rotation_flows` pre-aggregates per (entity, ticker), collapsing internal sub-CIK offsetting flows; `positions_changed` shifts on rare (entity, ticker) rows where `active_flow` was NULL (typically c.shares=0 carriers). Net flows preserved under any GROUP BY granularity; gross-flow shrinkage is structural. Fully documented in the function docstring. **Bonus fix:** the pre-rewrite SQL had a latent BinderException on `active_only=True` (referenced `c.entity_type` on a CTE that did not project the column); only `active_only=False` callers existed in prod, so it was never observed. New parent path supports `active_only=True` correctly via `peer_rotation_flows.entity_type`; fund path retains the bug since no caller uses level='fund' + active_only=True. `npm run build` passes (1.66s). `pre-commit run` passes on all touched files (ruff + pylint + bandit). All 8 `tests/smoke/` cases pass. **perf-P1 part 2 (`cohort_by_ticker_from`) remains open.** |

| 2026-04-26 | **pk-enforce ŌĆö migration 020 declares PRIMARY KEY on 21 L3/L4 tables** | New `scripts/migrations/020_pk_enforcement.py`. DuckDB has no syntax for adding a PK clause to an existing table's canonical DDL (`ALTER TABLE ... ADD PRIMARY KEY` bolts it on outside the stored CREATE TABLE and refuses while any index exists; cf. migration 011 preamble). The migration takes the stronger path: per table, snapshot via `CREATE TABLE <t>_pk_tmp AS SELECT *`, drop indexes + the original, re-execute the captured `duckdb_tables().sql` with `, PRIMARY KEY (cols)` injected before the closing paren (preserves every default, NOT NULL, sequence-default `nextval(...)` exactly), `INSERT INTO <t> SELECT * FROM <t>_pk_tmp`, recreate every index, drop the snapshot. Each per-table block is a transaction; idempotent across retries (PK probe short-circuits + defensive `_pk_tmp` cleanup). Cleanup pass: 1 dup row removed from `cik_crd_links` (kept higher match_score sibling of cik=`0001132708`/crd=`107138`). `entity_current` (only user-defined view, references entities/aliases/classification_history/rollup_history) dropped + recreated around the rebuild. **21 PKs declared:** market_data(ticker), adv_managers(crd_number), filings(accession_number), filings_deduped(accession_number), cik_crd_direct(cik,crd_number), parent_bridge(cik), entities(entity_id), entity_identifiers(identifier_type,identifier_value,valid_from), entity_relationships(relationship_id), entity_aliases(entity_id,alias_name,alias_type,valid_from), entity_classification_history(entity_id,valid_from), entity_overrides_persistent(override_id), entity_identifiers_staging(staging_id), entity_relationships_staging(id), investor_flows(ticker,period,rollup_type,rollup_entity_id), ticker_flow_stats(ticker,quarter_from,quarter_to,rollup_type), holdings_v2(row_id), fund_holdings_v2(row_id), beneficial_ownership_v2(row_id), cik_crd_links(cik,crd_number), entity_rollup_history(entity_id,rollup_type,valid_from,valid_to). v2 row_id sequences pre-flight verified ahead of MAX(row_id) ŌĆö `holdings_v2_row_id_seq` 101,770,777 vs MAX 98,564,908; `fund_holdings_v2_row_id_seq` 79,134,431 vs MAX 79,134,430; `beneficial_ownership_v2_row_id_seq` 220,997 vs MAX 220,996 ŌĆö so the recreated tables' inline `DEFAULT(nextval('<t>_row_id_seq'))` continues issuing non-colliding ids. Heaviest tables: investor_flows 18.6M rows (44.5s), holdings_v2 12.3M rows + 6 idx (44.9s), fund_holdings_v2 14.1M rows + 6 idx (44.8s). Total wall **137.7s**. Pre-commit clean (ruff/pylint/bandit/tracker-staleness all PASS); `pytest tests/smoke/ -v` 8/8. Schema stamp `020_pk_enforcement` at 2026-04-26 08:18 UTC. **`other_managers` deferred:** original spec proposed PK(accession_number, sequence_number, other_cik) with "delete 19 dups", but pre-flight surfaced 5,518 NULL `other_cik` rows (DuckDB rejects NULL in PK columns), and the "19" arithmetic only matches grouping on (accession_number, sequence_number). Decision pushed to a separate session ŌĆö likely PK(accession_number, sequence_number) with 19-row dedupe, but needs an explicit call. |

| 2026-04-23 | **hygiene-ticket-numbering ŌĆö codify retire-forever rule + audit script** | Branch `hygiene-ticket-numbering`. Two-file change. (1) `docs/REVIEW_CHECKLIST.md` ŌĆö new `## Ticket Number Discipline` section. Hard rule: ticket numbers (INF/DM/BL/mig-/int-/obs-/sec-/ops-/w2-/p2-/conv-/D/S) are monotonically increasing; once assigned, retired forever. Qualifier-suffix convention (INF40a/INF40b, DM15d/DM15e) codified for decompositions under an existing parent. Reviewer check documented: run `python3 scripts/audit_ticket_numbers.py` before approving PRs that open new tickets. (2) `scripts/audit_ticket_numbers.py` (~260 LOC) ŌĆö scans every `*.md` under the repo (skips `.claude`, `.git`, `retired/`, `snapshots/`, `superpowers/`, `node_modules/`, `dist/`, `build/`, `venv/`, `__pycache__/`, `coverage/`) for ticket references matching `(INF|DM|BL|mig-|int-|obs-|sec-|ops-|w2-|p2-|conv-)\d+[a-z]?`. Capped at number Ōēż999 to avoid collision with CIKs / series IDs. Emits prefix usage + gap report (e.g. `INF  count=21  range=[1..47]  gaps: [2,5,6,...]`) and a candidate-reuse block ŌĆö groups occurrences by normalized title (phase markers p0/p1/`Phase 0`/phase-suffix-in-filename stripped as stopwords; workflow-stage suffixes `-export`/`-apply`/`-dedup`/`-impl`/`-design` collapsed). Only "strong" definition lines count as reuse: `# heading`, `| **TICKET** | ...` table rows, or `- **TICKET**` bullets; parenthetical cross-ref headings (`## sec-07 Ōłź sec-08 disjoint`) explicitly filtered. `--strict` exits 1 on any candidate; default behavior is informational. Context: 2026-04-23 `build-fund-classes-rewrite` session discovered INF40 had been reused for two unrelated items (BLOCK-L3-SURROGATE-ROW-ID closed 2026-04-22 + entity-CTAS closed 2026-04-23). Disambiguation in prose is not enough ŌĆö grep and commit messages stay ambiguous forever. Audit against current tree surfaces **52 candidate-reuse clusters** for human review; the bulk are legitimate phase-splits (p0/p1 investigation ŌåÆ findings ŌåÆ implementation) and workflow stages (int-21-export ŌåÆ int-21-dedup ŌåÆ int-21-apply), not true reuse. |

| 2026-04-13 | **BL-10 ŌĆö 4 broken Excel exports (q6/q10/q11/q15) fixed** | Commit `9ea3557`. Root cause: the extractor in `api_export` (`scripts/api_register.py`) only handled dict responses with `positions` or `rows` keys. q6/q10/q11 are multi-list dicts; q15 is `list[1]` wrapping nested lists + a nested dict. The whole structure was being passed into openpyxl which choked on dict-as-row iteration and nested list cell values. **Fix:** new `build_excel_multisheet(sheets)` helper in `scripts/export.py` taking `{sheet_name: list[dict] | dict}` ŌåÆ one formatted sheet per entry. Sheet name sanitization (31-char cap, Excel-illegal char stripping, collision suffixes). Cell writer defensively str()s any list/dict the flattener misses. `api_export` detects multi-table shapes at runtime: (a) dict without `positions`/`rows` ŌåÆ one sheet per key; (b) `list[1]` with list/dict-valued fields ŌåÆ Overview sheet for scalars + one sheet per nested list/dict. Single-sheet path (q1, q2, q7, q16) unchanged. Verified: q6ŌåÆ5 sheets (activist_13d, passive_5pct, history, activist_13f, short_interest), q10ŌåÆ2 (new_entries, exits), q11ŌåÆ2 (same), q15ŌåÆ3 (Overview, quarters, coverage); all xlsx magic bytes `504b0304`; openpyxl round-trip load succeeds.
